7/6/21, 15:28 - Shri Om CSE C: *Cheating rule no 1:* 

Jo answer btayega woh question ka thoda part bhi likhega. Kyuki questions aur answers dono shuffle ho rhe hain. 

*Cheating rule no 2:* 

Phone se na dena nhi toh cheating aur mushkil ho jaayegi. Kyuki tb tm kahi aur dekh nhi paaoge. Aur phone me kuch change bhi ni kr paaoge. Phone ki jagah laptop use kro. Jisse ki phone se cheating kr sako. 

*Cheating rule no 3:*

 Chasme na phno. Agar thoda bhi dikhta hai chasme ke bina toh na phno. Nhi toh laptop ki screen aur phone ki screen dono chasme pe reflect hogi jise proctor dekh lega.

*Cheating rule no 4:* 

Proctor ek saath 50 logo ko dekhega aur woh bhi apni laptop ki screen pe. Iska mtlb yeh hai ki agar bhut jyada idhar udhar nhi kr rhe ho toh woh dekh ni paayega. Isliye normally sara kaam krna hai.

7/16/21, 17:47 - Sanjay Kr Singh Cse C: ATTENTION DEAR STUDENTS:
It is mandatory requirement to get yourself registered at AKTU ERP for appearing at the end term university examinations. AKTU has opened the registration process for B. Tech. I year students from 15 - 25 JULY 2020. Without registration, it will not be possible to appear at the university examinations. It is required for the students to complete their registration at AKTU ERP by the stipulated date.

Follow the given steps to complete the registration process:

1) Visit at aktu.ac.in
2) Click the tab - AKTU ERP
3) Enter user ID - Your roll no.
4) Enter Password- Password created by you at the time of filling examination form ( if not able to open/forget, please send a mail to studentsupport@abes.ac.in)
5) After entering password, you will reach at student "Student's portal"
6) Then click " Online Exam Credential" (see attached screen shot).
7) You will find your User ID, Password & URL to complete the registration for University exam.
8) Click the URL
9) You will find "Examination Registration Form" alongwith all your details.
10) Click "Proceed Application". (Do not make any change in any field/subjects).
11) Please complete the further processing as per direction given after there.

NOTE: STUDENTS TO ENSURE TO USE THE SAME DEVICE WHILE TAKING THE TEST AS USED TO COMPLETE THE REGISTRATION PROCEDURE. 

*In case of any difficulty/issue, please contact Mr. Nitin Manglik (9870829210) or send a mail at studentsupport@abes.ac.in.

Dear student,

As the pandemic recedes, we are very hopeful of beginning offline classes from the new academic session 2021-22. However, the final decision with respect to mode of classes shall be based on directions of the University and the Government.

The classes for the new academic session will start from September 13, 2021.The payment of academic fee towards registrations for the Odd Semester of the Academic Year 2021-22 is to be done by September10, 2021.Students are to pay the fee through Demand Draft or follow the following steps to deposit/transfer the College academic fee online and download the receipt of the payment made:

1.Login to you user account on ERP (Edumarshal.comor https://akgecerp.edumarshal.com)

2.      Go to Payment History

3.      Go to Pay Online

4.      Click on Pay (You will be navigated to your online Bank Portal)

To generate receipt of the fee payment made:

1.      Go to Payment History

2.      Download the receipt

Best wishes for physical opening of the College and good learning during the coming academic session.

  

(Dr. R. K. Agarwal)

Director General

8/25/21, 14:01 - Mehta Cs C: Dear All,
This is to inform you that ‘Stambh’-The Women Progress Cell ABES EC Ghaziabad under the banner of Mission Shakti (an AKTU initiative) provides the students an opportunity to participate in a competition of Poster making on the theme given below-
"Respect Women”
or 
“Women Safety against Violence”
A woman or girl should basically be respected first as a human being. Like any other human being, she must be valued by virtue of her merits and character and not by her physical appearance. The inner strength that each woman has should be believed, respected, valued and encouraged.
A woman is there is every part of a man throughout his life in the form of mother, sister, wife and daughter. We should respect other girls with dignity like how we respect and treat our family women. Women must be protected against social evils like rape, child and forced marriage, violence, slavery etc.
The best way to respect a woman is to respect her dignity, love, belief and by providing confidence, encouragement and moral support when needed. 
It is the time that together we own the responsibility and make each daughter and son of our country understand that the progress of our country rests on our shoulders as a whole and not on the shoulders of boys and girls, men or women.
It is rightly said "Be the change you want to see in others”. So, this comes to you as a platform to express your ideas through Posters on the topic- “Respect Women”
Details of the competitions: Participants can submit poster on any one of the topics ‘Respect Women’ OR ‘Women safety against violence’.
Event: Poster Making
Date of poster submission: 29/08/2021
Time: 12.30 pm
All entries will be received through Registration form (Poster will be uploaded in the registration form. Poster image must have student name, branch and year)
Registration Link: Kindly get yourself registered through the link below
https://forms.office.com/Pages/ResponsePage.aspx?id=Dn_YOpMfvUGU9ILDfZcciHkoj8oGY_1PrdUjPwPKQv5UQUNINlFVTkI5WDMyM09MVDY5VUdGSVo1MC4u
The winner entries will be provided with certificates. 
Rules and regulations for making Poster 
•	Drawing / painting must be on paper of A3 size (297 x 420 mm) or A2 size (420 x 594 mm). 
•	Acceptable tools of drawing / painting include pencil, crayon, water colour, oil paint etc. Photographs, wires, and other 3D objects are not acceptable. The completed artwork must be on a flat piece of paper.
•	Only one entry per person is allowed.
•	The drawing / painting must not represent any particular individual, organization, or brand name and must not depict any religious theme. 
•	The given theme "theme name" should be the main focus of the poster.
•	 No text (including theme title, name, etc) should be written on the front of the poster.
A poster should be an individual effort of the participant.
Event Coordinators: Dr. Manishi Mishra-9873533079 & Ms. Nandita Goyal-8130157451

8/27/21, 12:00 - Mehta Cs C: 📃 *_Word Your Way Out_* 📃

🎀"Don't ever diminish the power of words
 Words move hearts and the heart moves limbs."🎀

*Minerva- The Literary Society of ABESEC* is here with an engaging event that puts your skills to test and checks how strong your hold on language is. So be ready for some word-plays.

📜 *Event Details-* 📜

🗓️ *Date: 5/09/2021 and 6/09/2021* 

⭐ _The event will be conducted in three rounds._
 
🔷️ *Round 1- Rookie*

Date: 5th September, 2021
Time: 4:00 PM
Platform: Kahoot 

There will be a quiz of 24 questions involving a set of idioms, proverbs and riddles. Only top scorers will make it to the second round.🔏

🔷️ *Round 2- Spell to Tell*

Date: 5th September, 2021
Platform: Gmeet
Time: Post conclusion of Round 1

It is a Spell Bee. At this level, a total of 5 questions will be asked. Participants will be asked to spell words with difficulty increasing with every word. 2 marks will be awarded for each correct answer and -1 mark for a wrong answer. The sum total of points obtained by each participant in the 5 questions will be considered as their score for this round. On the basis of their scores from the start, the selected participants will advance for the final round. 💬🐝

🔷️ *ROUND 3- Climax*

Date: 6th September, 2021
Platform: Gmeet
Time: 4:00 PM

Ever wondered what could have happened if your favorite series ended differently? A character you crave to meet, comes alive?
Well, we have something for you all.

The participants will be asked to speak their mind on a given topic related to the cinematic world, made available to them only a few hours before the final round commences.🗣

The winner will be awarded a cash prize. 💸

⚙️ *Registration Fee: Rs. 20 per candidate* ⚙️

https://www.instagram.com/abesec.litsoc/

📧minerva.club@abes.ac.in

10/14/21, 17:44 - Mehta Cs C: *Hola Geeks! 🤓*
*GeeksforGeeks ABESEC Chapter* is back with the 🔥 *Recruitment Drive 2.1* 🔥 which was long-awaited. We’re recruiting for some technical positions through a fun tech-fest named *“Hacktoberfest 2021”*.
👉 Hacktoberfest, in its 8th year, is a month-long celebration of open source software being run by DigitalOcean. We invite you all to join open-source software enthusiasts, beginners, and the developer community by contributing to open-source projects. 

😃If you want to start your journey in Open Source and have struggled to find repos to contribute to, start today and get an opportunity to get recruited in one of the best technical clubs of our college.

🔹Any student who will commit code changes in any of the below-mentioned repositories or any other Open Source repos with more than 50 contributors, will be given a chance to sit for a Direct Interview, to be a part of the GFG Student chapter of ABESEC. 🥳
If you complete the Hacktoberfest 2021 Challenge, you’ll get a limited-edition T-shirt🤩🔥
(Top 70k people are only eligible for the T-Shirt)

🏅Rewards:-
*4 Code Based PR - Hacktoberfest T-shirt*
*3 Code Based PR - GFG Student Chapter of ABESEC interview*
*2 Code Based PR - MLSA certificate with Microsoft logo*

📝NOTE – You can sign up anytime between October 1 and October 31. Just be sure to sign up on the official Hacktoberfest website for your pull requests to count.

Catch all relevant links regarding the fest on: 
https://linktr.ee/geeksforgeeks_abesec

10/18/21, 16:08 - Ritik Cs C: #include<stdio.h>

void main()
{
    int n,m,p,q;
    scanf("%d%d%d%d",&m,&n,&p,&q);
    int i=1,g=1;
    
    for(i=1;(i<=m||i<=n||i<=p||i<=q);i++)
    {
        if(m%i==0&&n%i==0&&p%i==0&&q%i==0)
        {
            g=i;
        }
    }

printf("Greateest integer is %d",g);
}

A Very Happy Gandhi Jayanti !!🎊🎉
Mahatma Gandhi Ji once said *"The future of India lies in its villages"*

This was the dream of the father of the nation Mahatma Gandhi that real India is residing in rural areas and their development must be our top priority. On this special occasion of Gandhi Jayanti the *Unnat Bharat Abhiyan (UBA) wing of ABESEC*, which is a subdivision of a flagship program by the Ministry of Human Resource Development and IIT-D that aims to enrich Rural India, is going to organise a Virtual IdeaThon *SAMADHAN from 2 OCT 2021*.

🌟Winners will get prizes worth 2000 INR.

📍*The candidate can make a team of 2 members.*
📍Candidates have to register through the Proposal document (word file) and PPT(attached with        this mail).
📍*Registrations start on 2 Oct 2021 and will end on 18 Oct 2021, 11:59 PM.*
📍The Proposal Guidelines and samples along with possible projects/ sanctioned projects ( one can choose from this list also) is attached.

Date: 2/10/2021 Onwards*

int main()
{

    printf("\nEnter the size of first array ");

    scanf("%d",&n2);

    for(int i=0;i<n1;i++)      //Array Initialized
    {
       scanf("%d",&a[i]);
       c[i]=a[i];
    }
    int k=n1;
    printf("\nEnter the sorted array elements");
    for(int i=0;i<n2;i++)      //Array Initialized
    {
        scanf("%d",&b[i]);
        c[k]=b[i];
        k++;
    }
    printf("\nThe merged array..\n");
    for(int i=0;i<n3;i++)
    printf("%d ",c[i]);        //Print the merged array

    for(int i=0;i<n3;i++)         //Sorting Array
    {
        int temp;
        for(int j=i+1; j<n3 ;j++)
        {
            if(c[i]<c[j])
            {
                temp=c[i];
                c[i]=c[j];
                c[j]=temp;
            }
        }

int main() {

  int i, n;

  // initialize first and second terms
  int t1 = 0, t2 = 1;

  // initialize the next term (3rd term)
  int nextTerm = t1 + t2;

  // get no. of terms from user
  printf("Enter the number of terms: ");
  scanf("%d", &n);

  // print the first two terms t1 and t2
  printf("Fibonacci Series: %d, %d, ", t1, t2);

  // print 3rd to nth terms
  for (i = 3; i <= n; ++i) {
    printf("%d, ", nextTerm);
    t1 = t2;
    t2 = nextTerm;
    nextTerm = t1 + t2;
  }

  return 0;
}

Categories:-

6. People using unfair means will be automatically disqualified without any prior notice.

7. You can submit your entry by responding to the attached google form (this form will only accept a single response).

8. No entries allowed after 12th November midnight(11:59 PM)

Hello everyone,😊

🌟We are from HUHC ( Help Us to Help Child), a Non-Government Organization that works for the upliftment and education of underprivileged children.
 
We work along with other members like you all so that we can help them to achieve their true potential and provide them with the best possible opportunities which we can provide from our sides.

We would like you all to come forward for such a noble cause. It would hardly cost you an hour a week. 

We are willingly looking forward to all of your participation.

For more info please visit website:-http://huhcindia.org/

Anushka- 9568654005

*Thank you*
*Keep Helping*
*Keep Smiling*

 With regards,
*Team HUHC*
